<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='9',FILE='C:\jms\109192\15-20459-1\task7697181\20459-1-bi.htm',USER='109192',CD='Dec  8 00:05 2015' -->

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of Contents</a></font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:black;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">SIP Litigation -</font></b><font color="black" style="color:black;"> On February&nbsp;4, 2005, the Litigation Trust commenced lawsuits both in the United States District Court for the Northern District of Illinois (the &#147;Federal SIP Lawsuits&#148;) and in the Circuit Court of Cook County Illinois (the &#147;State SIP Lawsuits&#148;) to collect on&nbsp;the remaining&nbsp;SIP Participants&#146; promissory notes.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><u><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:black;font-size:10.0pt;">Federal SIP Lawsuits:</font></u><font color="black" style="color:black;"> The Litigation Trust filed and a federal district court judge entered summary judgments (and amended judgments) against all but one of the SIP Participants who were defendants in the federal cases (the &#147;Federal SIP Defendants&#148;) on their respective SIP promissory notes,&nbsp;and the Litigation Trust commenced collection actions against them.&nbsp;Additionally, the federal district court judge entered orders&nbsp;directing that certain CDRs and related proceeds held by the estate of Comdisco,&nbsp;Inc. and Computershare (f/k/a BNY Mellon) (holder of CDRs) on behalf of those Federal SIP Defendants be turned over to the Litigation Trust.&nbsp; Pursuant to such orders, the Company turned over CDRs and related proceeds and will continue to do so if additional orders are entered.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:38.25pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Following a series of motions, hearings and the completion of discovery</font>, at a hearing on July&nbsp;8, 2013, Judge Robert Gettleman set a trial date for September&nbsp;23, 2013.&#160; The trial&#146;s actual start date was September&nbsp;24, 2013 and the witness testimony and evidentiary phase was substantially completed on October&nbsp;10, 2013.&#160; On March&nbsp;27, 2014 the post-trial briefing was completed by the parties. The judge heard oral arguments on April&nbsp;16, 2014 and took the matter under advisement.&#160; On October&nbsp;21, 2014, the judge orally ruled and entered judgment in favor of the Federal SIP Defendants.&#160; The basis of the judge&#146;s ruling and judgment was his finding that both the bank and the Company committed an arranging violation under the applicable margin lending regulations.&#160; Therefore, the judge ruled that the promissory notes were void and unenforceable.&#160; <font color="black" style="color:black;">On October&nbsp;29, 2014, the litigation trustee filed an appeal of the judgment to the United States Court of Appeals for the Seventh Circuit.&nbsp; On November&nbsp;20, 2014, the Federal SIP Defendants filed a Notice of Appeal of the October&nbsp;21, 2014 judgment and of an order entered on August&nbsp;12, 2013. See update in &#147;Litigation Trust Reports and Settlement Update&#148; below.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:35.25pt;"><u><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:black;font-size:10.0pt;">State SIP Lawsuits:</font></u><font color="black" style="color:black;"> The Litigation Trust filed summary judgments against all of the SIP Participants who are defendants in the state cases (the &#147;State SIP Defendants&#148;, and, together with the Federal SIP Defendants, the &#147;SIP Defendants&#148;). Three of the State SIP Defendants filed Cross Motions for Summary Judgment.&nbsp; A hearing in the Circuit Court of Cook County on all of the summary judgment motions in the state cases was held on May&nbsp;12, 2010, and the judge granted the summary judgments in favor of the Litigation Trust and denied the various motions for summary judgments filed by the State SIP Defendants.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size:10.0pt;">After a series of hearings, motions and counter-motions, amended pleadings and individual bankruptcies and settlements, the remaining </font><font color="black" style="color:black;">State SIP Defendants</font></font> and the litigation trustee entered into an agreed Stipulation And Order (the &#147;Stipulation&#148;) which, among other things, stays the trials in the state cases pending the resolution and any appeal of the trial in the federal&nbsp;cases.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><u><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:black;font-size:10.0pt;">Litigation Trust Report and Settlement update:</font></u><font color="black" style="color:black;"> By early 2005,&nbsp;sixty-nine SIP Participant&#146;s promissory notes were transferred to the Litigation Trust.&nbsp;&nbsp;As reported in various Status Reports of Comdisco Litigation Trustee, of the sixty-nine SIP Participants:&#160; forty-one&nbsp;have settled or otherwise resolved their obligation; twelve have filed personal bankruptcy; and, sixteen&nbsp;notes remain outstanding (five in the federal court and eleven in the state court).</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:38.25pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:black;font-size:10.0pt;">On October&nbsp;1, 2015, the litigation trustee and the Company entered into a Global Settlement Agreement&nbsp;(the &#147;GSA&#148;) with the remaining SIP Defendants. Such settlement under the GSA does not have a material impact of the consolidated financial statements.&#160; </font><font color="black" style="color:black;">On October&nbsp;6, 2015, the&nbsp;litigation trustee filed with the United States Bankruptcy Court for the Northern District of Illinois Eastern Division a Motion seeking the entry of an order to (i)&nbsp;approve a proposed settlement with the remaining federal and state defendants who had executed promissory notes in connection with Comdisco,&nbsp;Inc.&#146;s Shared Investment Plan, (ii)&nbsp;approve the filing of the final report of the litigation trustee and (iii)&nbsp;upon the wind down of the Comdisco Litigation Trust and final disbursement of its net proceeds to the beneficiaries, terminate the Comdisco Litigation Trust and discharge the litigation trustee and the Comdisco Litigation Trust Advisory Board. </font><font color="black" style="color:black;">On November&nbsp;23, 2015, a hearing was held in the Bankruptcy court and the judge granted an order approving the Motion and set a hearing for April&nbsp;1, 2016.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For more details regarding the Litigation Trust and related proceedings, please refer to the Status Reports of Comdisco Litigation Trustee filed quarterly in the Bankruptcy court. Any proceeds collected by the Litigation Trust, net of expenses, will be considered Trust Assets and distributed in accordance with the Plan and the litigation trust agreement.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;">10<a name="PB_10_152924_7091"></a></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">ITEM 4.&#160; MINE SAFETY DISCLOSURES</font></b><a name="ITEM4_MINESAFETYDISCLOSURES_042101"></a></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Not applicable.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">PART&nbsp;II</font></b><a name="PARTII_042103"></a></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">ITEM 5. MARKET FOR REGISTRANT&#146;S COMMON EQUITY, RELATED STOCKHOLDER MATTERS AND ISSUER PURCHASES OF EQUITY SECURITIES</font></b><a name="ITEM5_MARKETFORREGISTRANTSCOMMON_042104"></a></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company&#146;s Common Stock currently trades on the OTCQB under the symbol &#147;CDCO&#148;. In addition, the CDRs currently trade on the OTCQB under the symbol &#147;CDCOR&#148;. OTCQB quotations reflect inter-dealer prices, without retail mark-up, markdown or commission and may not necessarily represent actual transactions.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Plan authorizes, but does not require, the issuance of additional shares of the Company&#146;s Common Stock to make distributions to holders of CDRs. The Company has historically chosen to distribute cash to holders of CDRs in lieu of shares of Common Stock (see discussion following for distributions made to holders of CDRs). More information on distributions to holders of CDRs can be found in a Registration Statement on Form&nbsp;8-A filed by the Company on August&nbsp;12, 2002 with the SEC and in the section Contingent Distribution Rights in Item 7, Management&#146;s Discussion and Analysis of Financial Condition and Results of Operations.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Common Stock</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As of December&nbsp;3, 2015, there were 224 shareholders of record of the Company&#146;s Common Stock. </font>In furtherance of the Global Settlement Agreement (the &#147;GSA&#148;), the Company will repurchase 26 shares of common stock from the litigation trustee at a discounted price of approximately $4.33 per share.&#160; These shares were acquired by the litigation trustee in the SIP Litigation.&#160; Shortly thereafter, the Company will cancel those shares.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.14%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>    </td>   </tr>  </table>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Contingent Distribution Rights</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Although the CDRs trade over-the-counter, for financial reporting purposes, the Company records CDRs as a liability under both the going concern and liquidation bases of accounting and as an operating expense under the going concern basis of accounting.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Plan entitled holders of CDRs to previously share at increasing percentages in the proceeds realized from the Company&#146;s assets based upon the present value of distributions to certain C-4 creditors in the bankruptcy estate of Comdisco,&nbsp;Inc. However, as of September&nbsp;30, 2015, the sharing percentage is 37%, which is the maximum sharing percent.&#160; As of the date of this filing, there were 1,840 holders of record of the Company&#146;s CDRs and there were 148,448,188 outstanding CDRs.</font>&#160; In furtherance of the settlement in the GSA, the Company will repurchase approximately 3,000,000 CDRs from the litigation trustee at a discounted purchase price of approximately $0.06898 per CDR.&#160; The CDRs were acquired by the litigation trustee in the SIP Litigation.&#160; Shortly after the repurchase, the Company will cancel those CDRs. The number of holders of CDRs may, or may not, be affected by such repurchase and cancellation.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company maintains sufficient cash reserves for operations and any increase in the estimated CDR liability relating to increases in the Company&#146;s net assets in liquidation and any future estimated net distributions from the Litigation Trust to the C-4 creditors.&#160; The outcome and the timing of the actual net distributions from the Litigation Trust will impact both the timing and the amount of future liquidating dividends and CDR payments.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As of October&nbsp;1, 2014, the Company has adopted the liquidation basis of accounting.&#160; The CDR liability is an amount that is calculated as Total Assets less Total Liabilities (excluding the CDR liability) times 37%.&#160; During the current period, the Company estimated an additional CDR liability in the amount of $370,000 (based on the likely anticipated distribution reported by the litigation trustee of Trust Assets in its supplement to the final report filed with the Bankruptcy court on October&nbsp;6, 2015) and is reflected on the Consolidated Statement of Net Assets in Liquidation as of September&nbsp;30, 2015 (Liquidation Basis) under Liabilities at Supplemental CDR Liability Due To Anticipated Litigation Trust Distribution.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:38.25pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Aggregate total distributions to the date of this report with respect to the CDRs were as follows (in thousands):</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Repurchases of Common Stock</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">There were no repurchases of Common Stock in the fourth quarter of fiscal 2015 or during the fiscal year 2015. The Company does not regularly repurchase shares nor does the Company have a share repurchase plan.</font>&#160; In furtherance of the settlement in the GSA, the Company will repurchase 26 shares of common stock from the litigation trustee at a discounted price of approximately $4.33 per share.&#160; These shares were acquired by the litigation trustee in the SIP Litigation.&#160; Shortly thereafter, the Company will cancel those shares.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">ITEM 6. SELECTED FINANCIAL DATA</font></b><a name="ITEM6_SELECTEDFINANCIALDATA_042108"></a></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Not applicable.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">ITEM 7. MANAGEMENT&#146;S DISCUSSION AND ANALYSIS OF FINANCIAL CONDITION AND RESULTS OF OPERATIONS</font></b><a name="ITEM7_MANAGEMENTSDISCUSSIONANDAN_042110"></a></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The following discussion and analysis should be read in conjunction with the Consolidated Financial Statements (in liquidation) and related notes included elsewhere in this Annual Report on Form&nbsp;10-K for the fiscal year ended September&nbsp;30, 2015. This discussion and analysis also contains forward-looking statements and should also be read in conjunction with the disclosures and information contained in the sections of this Annual Report on Form&nbsp;10-K entitled &#147;Disclosure Regarding Forward-Looking Statements&#148; and &#147;Risk Factors Relating to the Company.&#148;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company emerged from Chapter 11 bankruptcy proceedings on August&nbsp;12, 2002. The purpose of the Company is to sell, collect or otherwise reduce to money in an orderly manner the remaining assets of the corporation. Pursuant to the Company&#146;s First Amended Joint Plan of Reorganization (the &#147;Plan&#148;) and restrictions </font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;">13<a name="PB_13_153554_8627"></a></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade align="left" style="color:#010101;"></div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of Contents</a></font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">contained in the Company&#146;s Certificate of Incorporation (the &#147;Certificate&#148;), the Company is specifically prohibited from engaging in any business activities inconsistent with its limited business purpose.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:38.25pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company filed, on August&nbsp;12, 2004, a Certificate of Dissolution with the Secretary of State of the State of Delaware to formally extinguish Comdisco Holding Company,&nbsp;Inc.&#146;s corporate existence with the State of Delaware except for the purpose of completing the wind down contemplated by the Plan.&#160; Capitalized terms used but not defined in the Annual Report on Form&nbsp;10-K have the meanings as defined in the Plan.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Under the Plan, the Company was charged with, and has been, liquidating its assets. While there have been no changes either to the Plan, or the Company&#146;s obligations under it, the Company adopted ASU 2013-07, <i>Liquidation Basis of Accounting </i>as of October&nbsp;1, 2014 and accordingly determined that liquidation was imminent. Therefore, effective October&nbsp;1, 2014, the Company applied the liquidation basis&nbsp;of accounting on a prospective basis. </font>The liquidation basis of accounting requires the Company to estimate net cash flows from operations and to accrue all costs associated with implementing and completing the plan of liquidation and requires management to make estimates that affect the amounts reported in the consolidated financial statements and the related notes. &#160;Due to the adoption of the liquidation basis of accounting as of October&nbsp;1, 2014, the comparability of results of operations of current year periods to prior year periods is limited.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company is currently projecting December&nbsp;31, 2016 as the end date for its wind down of operations. It is anticipated that by this date the Company will have, among other things: finalized the settlement of the SIP, received the projected escrow funds from the Ebates transaction, reduced all of its assets to cash, resolved its final federal and state tax obligations, determined its final CDR liability (which will include the impact of the actual distribution by the Litigation Trust to the C-4 creditors), made distributions of all available cash to holders of its common stock and CDRs in the manner and priorities set forth in the Plan, cancelled such common stock and CDRs and completed all regulatory filings.&#160; Accordingly, it has made appropriate expense accruals for such time period in its calculation of Net Assets in Liquidation. However, the projected remaining wind down period could be either shortened or lengthened by other intervening matters not currently known to management.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">General</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company&#146;s operations continued to wind down during the fiscal year 2015. The Company&#146;s assets at September&nbsp;30, 2015 consist primarily of cash and cash-equivalents, receivable from securities sold and other assets.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:40.3pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Equity Investments: The Company sold its remaining preferred stock holdings in private companies during the twelve months ended September&nbsp;30, 2015 for $433,000 and received net proceeds of $368,000 after Windspeed Acquisition Fund GP, LLC (&#147;Windspeed&#148;) management sharing of $65,000. Beginning October&nbsp;1, 2014, these investments were carried at the liquidation basis of accounting in the Company&#146;s consolidated statement of net assets in liquidation.&#160; During April&nbsp;2015, </font>the Company discovered that it&nbsp;had received 1,499 shares in NxStage Medical,&nbsp;Inc., a publicly traded company.&#160; The shares were received in 1999 as part of a product spinoff from a former customer who subsequently went out of business.&nbsp; During the twelve months ended September&nbsp;30, 2015, these shares were sold for approximately $22,600 before Windspeed management sharing of approximately $3,400.&#160; As of September&nbsp;30, 2015, the Company does not own any shares in publicly traded companies.&#160; See Notes 6 and 10 of Notes to Consolidated Financial Statements (in Liquidation).</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company&#146;s estimate of the fair value of its private company investments were made in consultation with Windspeed, a professional management group, which the Company engaged in February&nbsp;2004 to manage the Company&#146;s equity investments on an ongoing basis.&#160; Windspeed shares in the net receipts from the sale of the Company&#146;s equity investments at a set percentage in certain designated portions of the portfolio of companies.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Windspeed management agreement was extended on April&nbsp;5, 2011 (with an effective date of February&nbsp;21, 2011) until February&nbsp;20, 2013 (the &#147;Initial Extension&#148;).&#160; The Windspeed management agreement was subsequently extended effective February&nbsp;21, 2013 through February&nbsp;20, 2015 and again extended effective February&nbsp;12, 2015 through February&nbsp;12, 2017 (the &#147;Subsequent Extensions&#148;).&#160; Prior to the Initial Extension, Windspeed received fixed and declining management fees.&#160; Under the terms of the Initial and Subsequent Extensions, Windspeed is not, and will not, be paid any ongoing management fees.&#160; In lieu of such management fee </font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;">14<a name="PB_14_153658_7906"></a></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade align="left" style="color:#010101;"></div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size:10.0pt;">payment, 100% of any proceeds from certain designated companies in the portfolio will go to Windspeed.&#160; Realized and unrealized gains on the sale of equity investments are presented on a gross basis. Any management sharing amounts with Windspeed are included in</font>  </font>accrued professional fees.&#160; See Note 6 of Notes to Consolidated Financial Statements (in Liquidation) and &#147;Critical Accounting Policies&#148;.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As of September&nbsp;30, 2015, the Company did not own any shares in publicly-traded companies within Equity Investments as presented on the consolidated statement of net assets in liquidation.&#160; However, the Company held a limited number of securities in trust for a deferred compensation plan which are not available for distribution under the Plan.&#160; The following table summarizes the changes in the value of the Company&#146;s Equity Investments since September&nbsp;30, 2014 (in thousands):</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" width="98%" style="border-collapse:collapse;">
<tr>
<td width="66%" valign="top" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:66.96%;">
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 10.1pt;text-align:center;text-indent:-10.1pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>    </td>
<td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.56%;">
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>    </td>
<td width="12%" valign="bottom" style="border:none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:12.24%;">
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Public <br>   Companies<br>   (2)(3)</font></p>    </td>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">There is no assurance as to the amount the Company will ultimately realize on the receivable from securities sold which is subject to the risk factors discussed in Item 1A, &#147;Risk Factors&#148;, entitled &#147;Uncertainties Inherent in the Determination of Value of the Ebates Escrow.&#148;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Collections and recoveries</font></u>: As of September&nbsp;30, 2015, the Company had no significant potential collections and recoveries.&#160; Prior recoveries involved former lessees or debtors now in bankruptcy and against whom the Company had filed and was pursuing claims to maximize its recoveries.&#160; The Company&#146;s cost basis in these accounts was nominal.&#160; Additionally, the Company, periodically, recovers unclaimed property from various states.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The amount and timing of such collections and recoveries, if any, are subject to the risk factors discussed in Item 1A, &#147;Risk Factors&#148;, particularly the risk entitled &#147;Uncertainties in Collections and Recoveries.&#148;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Subsidiaries: The Company has significantly reduced the number of its domestic and international subsidiaries from ninety-four to two subsidiaries as of December&nbsp;3, 2015.&#160; To the extent that such subsidiaries were Reorganized Debtors, the Company has closed the related estates.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Trust Assets and Litigation Trust</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Under the Plan, the litigation trustee is solely responsible for collecting from any remaining SIP Participants who had not accepted the relief offer in the Plan. Any amounts, net of fees and expenses, collected by the litigation trustee whether by judgment or settlement are considered Trust Assets. The litigation trustee has filed periodic reports with the Bankruptcy court, including a final report filed on October&nbsp;6, 2015, and such reports provided and provide additional information on the collection efforts, any settlements and potential distributions of Trust Asset.&#160; The litigation trustee is solely responsible for distributing Trust Assets to C-4 Creditors under the Plan.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;">15<a name="PB_15_154053_3736"></a></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of Contents</a></font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During the current period, the Company estimated an additional CDR liability in the amount of $370,000 (based on the likely anticipated distribution reported by the litigation trustee of Trust Assets in its supplement to the final report filed with the Bankruptcy court on October&nbsp;6, 2015) and is reflected on the Consolidated Statement of Net Assets in Liquidation as of September&nbsp;30, 2015 (Liquidation Basis) under Liabilities at Supplemental CDR Liability Due To Anticipated Litigation Trust Distribution.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Emergence from Bankruptcy</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Since emerging from Chapter 11 bankruptcy proceedings on August&nbsp;12, 2002, the Company has, pursuant to the Plan, focused on the monetization of its remaining assets. Therefore, comparisons of quarter-to-quarter or year-to-year results of operations should not be relied upon as an indication of the Company&#146;s future performance.&#160; Capitalized terms used but not defined in this section shall have the meanings as defined in the Plan.&#160; Under the Plan, the Company was charged with, and has been, liquidating its assets. While there have been no changes either to the Plan, or the Company&#146;s obligations under it, the Company adopted ASU 2013-07, <i>Liquidation Basis of Accounting </i>as of October&nbsp;1, 2014 and accordingly, determined that liquidation was imminent. Therefore, effective October&nbsp;1, 2014, the Company applied the liquidation basis of accounting on a prospective basis.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">All funds generated from the Company&#146;s remaining asset portfolios are required by the Plan to be used to satisfy liabilities of the Company and, to the extent funds are available, to pay dividends on the Company&#146;s Common Stock and to make distributions with respect to the CDRs in the manner and priorities set forth in the Plan.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On February&nbsp;20, 2015, the Company issued a press release announcing that its Board of Directors had declared a cash dividend of $2.3455 per share on the outstanding shares of its Common Stock (an aggregate distribution of approximately $9,450,000).&#160; This was paid on March&nbsp;12, 2015 to common stockholders of record as of March&nbsp;2, 2015. &#160;Comdisco intends to treat the dividend distributions for federal income tax purposes as part of a series of liquidating distributions in complete liquidation of the Company</font>.&#160; The Company paid no dividends during the fiscal year ended September&nbsp;30, 2014.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On February&nbsp;20, 2015, the Company announced that it would make a cash payment of $0.03739 per CDR, (an aggregate payment of approximately $5,550,000).&#160;&#160; This was paid on March&nbsp;12, 2015 to CDR holders of record as of March&nbsp;2, 2015</font>.&#160; The Company made no payment to CDR holders during the fiscal year ended September&nbsp;30, 2014.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">See Item 1, &#147;General Terms of the Plan of Reorganization&#148; and Part&nbsp;II,&nbsp;Item 5, &#147;Market for Registrant&#146;s Common Equity, Related Stockholder Matters and Issuer Purchases of Equity Securities&#148;.&#160; Other than the estimated receivable from securities sold from the Ebates transaction, the Company expects to generate funds from the sale or collection of its remaining assets at a decreasing rate over time.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company maintains sufficient cash reserves for operations and any increase in the estimated CDR liability relating to increases in the Company&#146;s net assets in liquidation and any future estimated net distributions from the Litigation Trust to the C-4 creditors.&#160; The outcome and the timing of the actual net distributions from the Litigation Trust will impact both the timing and the amount of future liquidating dividends and CDR payments.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As of October&nbsp;1, 2014, the Company has adopted the liquidation basis of accounting.&#160; The CDR liability is an amount that is calculated as Total Assets less Total Liabilities (excluding the CDR liability) times 37%. During the current period, the Company estimated an additional CDR liability in the amount of $370,000 (based on the likely anticipated distribution reported by the litigation trustee of Trust Assets in its supplement to the final report filed with the Bankruptcy court on October&nbsp;6, 2015) and is reflected on the Consolidated Statement of Net Assets in Liquidation as of September&nbsp;30, 2015 (Liquidation Basis) under Liabilities at Supplemental CDR Liability Due To Anticipated Litigation Trust Distribution.&#160; See below for &#147;Critical Accounting Policies&#148; and Item 1A, &#147;Risk Factors&#148; for a discussion of the &#147;Impact of Recoveries by Litigation Trust on the Company&#146;s Obligation To Make Payments in Respect of Contingent Distribution Rights&#148; and &#147;</font>Uncertainties Inherent in the CDR Liability Calculation.&#148;</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company has material restrictions on its ability, and does not expect, to make significant investments in new or additional assets. The Company continually evaluates opportunities for the orderly sale and collection of its remaining assets.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;">16<a name="PB_16_154109_9621"></a></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade align="left" style="color:#010101;"></div>
</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='16',FILE='C:\JMS\109206\15-20459-1\task7697032\20459-1-bk.htm',USER='109206',CD='Dec  7 21:29 2015' -->

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of Contents</a></font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company is currently projecting December&nbsp;31, 2016 as the end date for its wind down of operations. It is anticipated that by this date the Company will have, among other things: finalized the settlement of the SIP, received the projected escrow funds from the Ebates transaction, reduced all of its assets to cash, resolved its final federal and state tax obligations, determined its final CDR liability (which will include the impact of the actual distribution by the Litigation Trust to the C-4 creditors), made distributions of all available cash to holders of its common stock and CDRs in the manner and priorities set forth in the Plan, cancelled such common stock and CDRs and completed all regulatory filings.&#160; Accordingly, it has made appropriate expense accruals for such time period in its calculation of Net Assets in Liquidation. However, the projected remaining wind down period could be either shortened or lengthened by other intervening matters not currently known to management.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Critical Accounting Policies</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company&#146;s consolidated financial statements are prepared in accordance with U.S. generally accepted accounting principles. Under the Plan, the Company was charged with, and has been, liquidating its assets. While there have been no changes either to the Plan, or the Company&#146;s obligations under it, the Company adopted ASU 2013-07, <i>Liquidation Basis of Accounting </i>as of October&nbsp;1, 2014 and accordingly, determined that liquidation was imminent. Therefore, effective October&nbsp;1, 2014, the Company applied the liquidation basis of accounting on a prospective basis.&#160; As such, the preparation of the fiscal year 2015 financial statements is under the liquidation basis of accounting which requires management to use estimates that affect reported amounts of assets and liabilities, revenues and expenses, and disclosure of contingent assets and liabilities.&#160; These estimates are subject to known and unknown risks, uncertainties and other factors that could materially impact the amounts reported and disclosed in the consolidated statement of net assets in liquidation.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The SEC issued Financial Reporting Release No.&nbsp;60, &#147;Cautionary Advice Regarding Disclosure About Critical Accounting Policies,&#148; which recommends that companies provide additional disclosure and analysis of those accounting policies considered most critical.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company believes the following to be the most critical judgment area in the application of its accounting policies:</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 56.9pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-20.9pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Future Cash Inflows and Future Outflows</u>: As of October&nbsp;1, 2014, the Company has adopted the liquidation basis of accounting on a prospective basis which requires the estimation of and accrual of all projected future cash inflows and future outflows associated with implementing and completing the plan of liquidation and requires management to make estimates that affect the amounts reported in the consolidated statements of net assets in liquidation and the related notes. Results could differ from these estimates and may affect the net assets in liquidation and actual cash flows.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The above listing is not intended to be a comprehensive list of all the Company&#146;s accounting policies. Please refer to the Company&#146;s annual Consolidated Financial Statements (in Liquidation) and notes thereto which contain the Company&#146;s significant accounting policies and other disclosures required by accounting principles generally accepted in the United States of America.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Basis of Presentation</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In this Annual Report on Form&nbsp;10-K, references to &#147;the Company,&#148; &#147;Comdisco Holding,&#148; &#147;we,&#148; &#147;us&#148; and &#147;our&#148; mean Comdisco Holding Company,&nbsp;Inc., its consolidated subsidiaries, including Comdisco,&nbsp;Inc., Comdisco Ventures Fund A, LLC (formerly Comdisco Ventures,&nbsp;Inc.), and its predecessors, except in each case where the context indicates otherwise. References to &#147;Comdisco,&nbsp;Inc.&#148; mean Comdisco,&nbsp;Inc. and its subsidiaries, prior to the Company&#146;s emergence from bankruptcy on August&nbsp;12, 2002, except where the context indicates otherwise.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Recent Developments</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Bankruptcy Proceeding</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Status Hearings: </font></u>&#160;The Company continues to appear before the Bankruptcy court from time to time to clarify and administer matters related to the Plan and the wind down of the operations of the Company.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;">17<a name="PB_17_154122_8715"></a></p>

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='17',FILE='C:\JMS\109206\15-20459-1\task7697032\20459-1-bk.htm',USER='109206',CD='Dec  7 21:29 2015' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of Contents</a></font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">L</font></b><b>itigation Trust Ongoing Litigation</b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:black;font-size:10.0pt;">The Plan and the litigation trust agreement provided that, under certain circumstances, subrogation rights that the Company may have against the SIP Participants and their respective promissory notes be placed in a trust for the benefit of the C-4 creditors (the &#147;Trust Assets&#148;).&#160; Under the Plan, the Litigation Trust is solely responsible for collection of amounts due on the promissory notes of the SIP Participants who did not accept the SIP Relief (as defined in the Plan).&#160; The Company has a limited indemnification obligation to the litigation trustee under the litigation trust agreement.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:black;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">SIP Litigation:</font></b><font color="black" style="color:black;">&#160; On February&nbsp;4, 2005, the Litigation Trust commenced lawsuits both in the United States District Court for the Northern District of Illinois (the &#147;Federal SIP Lawsuits&#148;) and in the Circuit Court of Cook County Illinois (the &#147;State SIP Lawsuits&#148;) to collect on&nbsp;the remaining&nbsp;SIP Participants&#146; promissory notes.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><u><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:black;font-size:10.0pt;">Federal SIP Lawsuits:</font></u><font color="black" style="color:black;"> The Litigation Trust filed and a federal district court judge entered summary judgments (and amended judgments) against all but one of the SIP Participants who were defendants in the federal cases (the &#147;Federal SIP Defendants&#148;) on their respective SIP promissory notes,&nbsp;and the Litigation Trust commenced collection actions against them.&nbsp;Additionally, the federal district court judge entered orders&nbsp;directing that certain CDRs and related proceeds held by the estate of Comdisco,&nbsp;Inc. and Computershare (f/k/a BNY Mellon) (holder of CDRs) on behalf of those Federal SIP Defendants be turned over to the Litigation Trust.&nbsp; Pursuant to such orders, the Company turned over CDRs and related proceeds and will continue to do so if additional orders are entered.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:38.25pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Following a series of motions, hearings and the completion of discovery</font>, at a hearing on July&nbsp;8, 2013, Judge Robert Gettleman set a trial date for September&nbsp;23, 2013.&#160; The trial&#146;s actual start date was September&nbsp;24, 2013 and the witness testimony and evidentiary phase was substantially completed on October&nbsp;10, 2013.&#160; On March&nbsp;27, 2014 the post-trial briefing was completed by the parties. The judge heard oral arguments on April&nbsp;16, 2014 and took the matter under advisement.&#160; On October&nbsp;21, 2014, the judge orally ruled and entered judgment in favor of the Federal SIP Defendants.&#160; The basis of the judge&#146;s ruling and judgment was his finding that both the bank and the Company committed an arranging violation under the applicable margin lending regulations.&#160; Therefore, the judge ruled that the promissory notes were void and unenforceable.&#160; <font color="black" style="color:black;">On October&nbsp;29, 2014, the litigation trustee filed an appeal of the judgment to the United States Court of Appeals for the Seventh Circuit.&nbsp; On November&nbsp;20, 2014, the Federal SIP Defendants filed a Notice of Appeal of the October&nbsp;21, 2014 judgment and of an order entered on August&nbsp;12, 2013.&#160; See update in &#147;Litigation Trust Reports and Settlement Update&#148; below.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:35.25pt;"><u><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:black;font-size:10.0pt;">State SIP Lawsuits:</font></u><font color="black" style="color:black;"> The Litigation Trust filed summary judgments against all of the SIP Participants who are defendants in the state cases (the &#147;State SIP Defendants&#148;, and, together with the Federal SIP Defendants, the &#147;SIP Defendants&#148;). Three of the State SIP Defendants filed Cross Motions for Summary Judgment.&nbsp; A hearing in the Circuit Court of Cook County on all of the summary judgment motions in the state cases was held on May&nbsp;12, 2010, and the judge granted the summary judgments in favor of the Litigation Trust and denied the various motions for summary judgments filed by the State SIP Defendants.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size:10.0pt;">After a series of hearings, motions and counter-motions, amended pleadings and individual bankruptcies and settlements, the remaining </font><font color="black" style="color:black;">State SIP Defendants</font></font> and the litigation trustee entered into an agreed Stipulation And Order (the &#147;Stipulation&#148;) which, among other things, stays the trials in the state cases pending the resolution and any appeal of the trial in the federal&nbsp;cases.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><u><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:black;font-size:10.0pt;">Litigation Trust Reports and Settlement Update:</font></u><font color="black" style="color:black;"> By early 2005,&nbsp;sixty-nine SIP Participant&#146;s promissory notes were transferred to the Litigation Trust.&nbsp;&nbsp;As reported in various Status Reports of Comdisco Litigation Trustee, of the sixty-nine SIP Participants:&#160; forty-one&nbsp;have settled or otherwise resolved their obligation; twelve have filed personal bankruptcy; and, sixteen&nbsp;notes remain outstanding (five in the federal court and eleven in the state court).</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:black;font-size:10.0pt;">On October&nbsp;1, 2015, the litigation trustee and the Company entered into a Global Settlement Agreement&nbsp;(the &#147;GSA&#148;) with the remaining SIP Defendants.&#160; Such settlement under the GSA does not have a material impact on the consolidated financial statements.&#160; </font><font color="black" style="color:black;">On October&nbsp;6, 2015, the&nbsp;litigation trustee filed with the United States Bankruptcy Court for the Northern District of Illinois Eastern Division a motion (the &#147;Motion&#148;) seeking the entry of an order to (i)&nbsp;approve a proposed settlement with the remaining federal and state defendants who had executed promissory notes in connection with Comdisco,&nbsp;Inc.&#146;s Shared Investment Plan, (ii)&nbsp;approve the filing of the final report of the litigation trustee and (iii)&nbsp;upon the wind down of the Comdisco Litigation Trust and final disbursement of its net </font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:black;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font color="black" style="color:black;">18</font><a name="PB_18_154319_5439"></a></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade align="left" style="color:#010101;"></div>

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of Contents</a></font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:black;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:black;font-size:10.0pt;">proceeds to the</font>  <font color="black" style="color:black;">beneficiaries, terminate the Comdisco Litigation Trust and discharge the litigation trustee and the Comdisco Litigation Trust Advisory Board. </font><font color="black" style="color:black;">On November&nbsp;23, 2015, a hearing was held in the Bankruptcy court and the judge granted an order approving the Motion and set a hearing for April&nbsp;1, 2016.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For more details regarding the Litigation Trust and related proceedings, please refer to the Status Reports of Comdisco Litigation Trustee filed quarterly in the Bankruptcy court. Any proceeds collected by the Litigation Trust, net of expenses, will be considered Trust Assets and distributed in accordance with the Plan and the litigation trust agreement.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Records Destruction</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On June&nbsp;26, 2008, the Company obtained an order from the Bankruptcy court authorizing it to destroy or transfer certain of its stored paper and electronic records attributed to periods prior to January&nbsp;1, 1997.&#160; As of the date of this filing, the Company destroyed substantially all of those records. Pursuant to the GSA approved by the Bankruptcy court on November&nbsp;23, 2015, which became final on December&nbsp;8, 2015, the Company is authorized to destroy corporate records created prior to January&nbsp;1, 2008.&#160; After its review of their import in the bankruptcy process, the Company will commence such destruction of appropriate records.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Subsidiary Changes</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company&#146;s Canadian subsidiary was liquidated during the fiscal year ended September&nbsp;30, 2014.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Results of Operations</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Due to the adoption of the liquidation basis of accounting as of October&nbsp;1, 2014, the comparability of results of operations of current year periods to prior year periods is limited.&#160; Under the liquidation basis of accounting, the Company is required to present a statement of net assets in liquidation (which replaces the balance sheet) and a statement of changes in net assets in liquidation (which replaces the income statement).&#160; To the extent there are any changes in the Company&#146;s October&nbsp;1, 2014 initial estimates, there will be changes reflected in the Statement of Changes in Net Assets in Liquidation.&#160; As cash is received or paid, consistent with the Company&#146;s initial estimates, there will be no change to the Net Assets in Liquidation which is the amount expected to be available for eventual distribution to the common stockholders.&#160; However, any cash distribution to the common stockholders during a fiscal year would be shown as a change in Net Assets in Liquidation during such fiscal year.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Changes in Net Assets in Liquidation (Liquidation Basis) for the year ended September&nbsp;30, 2015</font></u></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of Contents</a></font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 57.0pt;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(A)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Reduction to the CDR liability in the twelve months ended September&nbsp;30, 2015 is a result of higher accrued estimated record storage and disposal costs in the liquidation and higher accrued liabilities for travel and legal fees.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 57.0pt;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(B)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Increase to the Supplemental CDR Liability due to Anticipated Litigation Trust Distribution is based on anticipated net distributions by the litigation trustee as reported in its supplement to the final report.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(C)&nbsp;</font> Increase in accrued liabilities for estimated future travel and legal fees.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(D)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Increase in the accrued estimated record storage and disposal costs in the liquidation is a result of the projected additional length of time to store and then ultimately dispose of the paper records and electronic records.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(E)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The Company paid a liquidating distribution to Common Stockholders on March&nbsp;12, 2015 for approximately $9,450,000.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Income Taxes</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">See Note 5 &#150; Income Taxes of Notes to Consolidated Financial Statements (in Liquidation) for details about the Company&#146;s income tax provision (benefit).</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company&#146;s U.S. federal taxes are impacted from its wind down activities, including the liquidation and repatriation of foreign assets.&#160; </font>During the fiscal year ended September&nbsp;30, 2015, the Company paid $211,000 as a result of alternative minimum tax (&#147;AMT&#148;) due on the taxable income generated from the gain on sale of equity investments.&#160; This amount was accrued upon the adoption of the liquidation basis of accounting as of October&nbsp;1, 2014.&#160; The Company also paid $15,000 in payments to the IRS and paid $75,000 in payments to the Illinois Department of Revenue related to the fiscal year ended September&nbsp;30, 2014.&#160; During the fiscal year ended September&nbsp;30, 2014, the Company recorded $185,000 U.S. tax expense and paid $18,000 estimated payments to the IRS and paid $ 77,000 in estimated payments to the Illinois Department of Revenue.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Net Assets in Liquidation</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As of September&nbsp;30, 2015, net assets in liquidation were approximately $18,042,000, or $4.48 per common share.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Net Earnings (Going Concern)</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Net earnings were approximately $855,000, or $0.21 per share-basic and diluted, for the fiscal year ended September&nbsp;30, 2014.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Off-Balance Sheet Arrangements</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company does not maintain any off-balance sheet arrangements, transactions, obligations or other relationships with unconsolidated entities that would be expected to have a material current or future effect upon the Company&#146;s financial condition or results of operations.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Liquidity and Capital Resources</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The liquidation basis of accounting requires the Company to estimate net cash flows from operations and to accrue all costs associated with implementing and completing the plan of liquidation and requires management to make estimates that affect the amounts reported in the consolidated financial statements in liquidation and the related notes.&#160; Actual results could differ from these estimates and may affect net assets in liquidation and actual cash flows.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company&#146;s liquidity generally depends on cash on hand.&#160; The Company&#146;s cash flow from operating activities is dependent on a number of variables, including, but not limited to, operating costs and expenses to affect the wind down, income tax obligations, and the ability of the Company to dispose or otherwise convert to cash its </font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;">20<a name="PB_20_154657_5250"></a></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade align="left" style="color:#010101;"></div>
</div>
